 karnataka ke skulon main maasoom bacchon ke khilaaf badhate yon aparaadhon ko rokane ke makasad se ek khaas task force karnataka main agle do-teen dinon main taiyaar ho jayega
 Karnataka Chief Minister Siddaramaiah said that we are going to set up a task force under the supervision of senior officials of the Ministry of Education, Women and Child Development, Police, Information and Transport Department
 ye task force skool main bacchon kii hifaazat ke liye disha-nirdesh tay karegaa
 It will be headed by Additional Chief Secretary level officer
 isse pehle karnataka hai court ne rajya sarkaar ko 7 navambar tak ek hai power samiti ke gathan kaa aadesh diya tha
 At the same time, it was also said that the government is not looking serious about the need to protect the children going to school
 hoicourt ne apane aadesh main saafe kaha he ki ye samiti jo disha-nirdesh taiyaar karegi use karnataka ke sabhi nagarpalika ke tahat aane vaale shaharon ke skulon main lagu kiya jayega, chaahe skool nijee hon, sarkari yaa sarkaar se anudaan praapt hon
 Recently, there have been three cases of sexual harassment in schools with innocent children in Bengaluru
 maamla jab hoicourt pahunchaa to police ne apni taraf se disha-nirdesh taiyaar kiye, lekin court isse santusht nahin tha
 The resentment of the people is increasing rapidly due to the loose attitude of the administration
 aise main ummid kii ja rahi he ki hoicourt kii dakhlandaji ke baad ek aisi vyavastha ban paaegi jiske baad bachche skulon main surakshit rah paaenge
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi (PM Modi) on Tuesday started his election campaign in Bihar, targeting the Congress and other parties involved in the grand alliance
 pradhanmantri (PM Modi)ne khud ko 'chaikidaar' bataate hue kaha ki aaj is chaukeedaar se mahamilawat or unke pairokaar va aatankwaad or uske madadgaar pareshaan hai
 That is why they are abusing the watchman
 piem (PM Modi)ne kaha ki aatankwaad, bhrashtachar, naksalwad se nekaniyat vaali sarkaar hi muqabla kar sakati he
 Those who live for power cannot work in the national interest
 aarakshan ke mudde par piem ne kaha ki kai log daraane kaa kaam kar rahe hai, parantu koi bhi ise samaapt nahin kar saktaa
 Addressing an election rally at Gandhi Maidan in Gaya, Modi said that a lot was yet to be done
 unhone kaha ki jo log 70 saalon main satta main rahakar sabakuch kar lene kaa daawa nahin kar sakate, to main to paanch saal main sabakuch karne kaa daawa kaise kar saktaa hum
 But i have to make constant efforts, which needs your support
 piem ne logon se kaha ki desh main jo bhi vikaas kaa kaary sarkaar kar pai he, vah aap sabhi ke sahyog ke kaaran ho saki he
 Before 2014, bombings were carried out by terrorists in the country, but where did they go after 2014? pehle bhi yahi khufia vibhaag or police thi
 The Prime Minister countered Omar Abdullah's statement by saying that there could be no two Prime Ministers in this country
 unhone kaha ki kursi tantra ke liye milavati log aise aatankwaadiyon ko chhod dete the
 During this time he also took a dig at the Congress for 'hindu terrorism' and said, "the great leaders, including the Congress, played a fake game of Hindu terrorism for this to not be investigated properly
" virodhiyon ko hamaari chaukeedaari se dikkat hui to mahamilavati log chaukeedaar ko tarah-tarah kii gaali de rahe hai
 But the whole world is appreciating the work of the watchman
 piem ne 'mahagathbandhan' ko 'mahamilavati' bataate hue kaha ki ye log desh main aatankiyon, naksaliyon ko bhi badhaava dete hai
 When we guarded the conspiracies of such great people, they started getting into trouble
 chaukeedaar achche nahin lagane lage
 People with disabilities are hated by workers
 upi main avaidh boojadkhaane band karne kii muhim se meet kaarobaariyon main hadakamp much gaya he
 Before the election, the BJP had promised to close illegal slaughterhouses in the resolution letter
 yogi adityanath ke siem banate hi bijepi ke is vaade ko or majbootee mil gai he
 From election rallies to other public forums, Yogi Adityanath has been advocating the closure of slaughterhouses
 yahi vajah he ki ravivaar ko jaise hi yogi ne siem pad kii shapath lee uske baad boojadkhaanon par gaaj girani shuru ho gai
 Slaughterhouses are being sealed in different areas of UP
 haalanki sarkaar kii taraf se aupchaarik taur par is sambandh main koi aadesh nahin diya gaya he
 Closing illegal slaughterhouses in UP may be a matter for the BJP to fulfill the electoral issue
 lekin aisa hone se lakhon logon ke rojgaar kaa sankat bhi khadaa ho jayega
 According to a report, currently 40 slaughterhouses are legal in UP
 ye wo boojadkhaane hai jinhen centre sarkaar kii agricultural andprocessd food products export dawalpment athurity(apeda) se baqayada license mila hua he
 Whereas according to a report, the number of illegal slaughterhouses in UP is more than three and a half hundred
 bataa den ki upi desh main bhens ke meet kaa sabase bada niryaatak he
 Talking about the crisis in western UP, a large number of slaughterhouses are run in Meerut, Ghaziabad and Aligarh districts
 meerut shahar main hi vaid boojadkhaanon kii aad main bade paimaane par avaidh boojadkhaane chalaae ja rahe hai
 Thousands of people are employed in these illegal slaughterhouses
 aise main agar ye boojadkhaane band kar die jate hai to badi taadaad main logon par rojgaar kaa sankat paidaa ho jayega
 Action is being taken to close illegal slaughterhouses in Varanasi also in Sankat Varanasi
 varanasi ke jaitpura ilaake main mangalvaar ko police ne ek avaidh boojadkhana band karaayaa
 a large number of people are also connected to the abattoirs here
 kareeb 15 hajaar logon kaa rojgaar boojadkhaanon se judaa he
 Most of these people are those who have been doing the work of cutting meat from the books
 aise main is kaam ke alaava unke paas rojgaar kaa vikalp bachataa najar nahin aata he
 Asarkanpur is considered the economic capital of UP on the leather trade
 kanpur se sabade bada kaarobaar chamade kaa hota he
 Leather belts to bags and shoes are made in Kanpur
 deshbhar main kaccha chamada bhi kanpur se jaataa he
 About $ 12 billion worth of leather goods is exported from Kanpur to foreign countries every year
 yahaan sirf 6 boojadkhaane vaid hai jabaki avaidh boojadkhaanon kii sankhya pachaas se zyada he
 About 50 crore meat trade is done daily from Kanpur alone
 kisaanon par asarboochdakhaanon ko band karne kaa faisla sirf kaarobaariyon yaa mazdooron ko hi prabhavit nahin karegaa
 It will also have a wider impact on farmers
 2012 ke pashudhan jansankhya ke anusaar upi main bhens or gaay kii taadaad main baari ijapha hua he
 The number of buffaloes increased by 28 percent compared to 2007 while the number of cows increased by 10 percent
 bina doodh vaali gaay or bhens ko paalna kisaan ke liye badi chunauti hoti he
 Generally, farmers keep the same cattle which are either used for farming or are milch
 baaki duusare maweshiyon ko kisaan bech dete hai
 Feeding such cattle is also considered a major crisis for farmers
 yahaan band hue boojadkhanapulice prashasan ne avaidh boojadkhaane band karaane shuru kar die hai
 On Monday, when police arrived to close an illegal meat shop in Gajraula, the shopkeeper tried to burn himself by adding kerosene
 haalanki police ne use turant daboch liya
 After this, two slaughterhouses were sealed in Allahabad on Tuesday
 jabaki gajiabad ke kelaa bhatta ilaake main police ne 15 boojadkhaane band karaae
 Closure of illegal child labor in UP will have a major impact on the public
 aise main yogi adityanath ko apane chunavi vaade puure karne ke saath is kadam se prabhavit janata ke liye rojgaar ke vikalp bhi talashne honge

 nyaayalay ne pichley maheene (27 agast) ashraf ko raashtrapati jaradaari ke khilaaf bhrashtachar ke maamalon ko phir se kholane ke liye swiss prashasan ko patr likhane hetu teen saptaah kaa samay diya tha
 The Prime Minister said that he had given Law Minister Farooq H

 nyaayalay ne agali sunwaayee par pradhanmantri ko upasthit hone se chhot de di

 According to the newspaper Dawn, the bench, however, said that the time for consultations was over and the government should now focus on writing letters
